posted:Posted February 17, 2024
msg:I decided to stay in Xichang for a few days during the Spring Festival very early, and after comparison, I chose the General Hotel. First, we are not on a family vacation, and we don't want the surrounding environment to be too lively. Although Jiangjunli is a commercial district, it is not a popular business district in Xichang. There are not many people during the Spring Festival. The facts also prove that this condition is met. The few days I stayed were very quiet; second, the General Museum of the General Hotel is the place I want to visit most on this trip. It is also a cultural relic that is not well known in Xichang. It is close to the water and the tower did not disappoint me.
It is worth mentioning that the service level of the hotel is very good compared with the whole Xichang. The fruit is changed every day, and afternoon tea, supper and bedtime desserts are arranged for guests every day. The Chinese and Western breakfast sets are also very rich... Miss Yang Jie, who has been in contact with me since the reservation, has meticulous and professional service and a friendly attitude. We drank tea in the teahouse of the museum and arranged afternoon tea for us. Thank you very much. In addition, the reception staff and concierge at the front desk are also very good.
In general, although the stay time is not long, the experience is still relatively good. Finally, I would like to give a small suggestion to the hotel: the rooms should be equipped with gauze curtains. In addition to filtering ultraviolet rays, more importantly, it can protect privacy.
